% Ans        : MultiAns
% File       : 0054
% Sub        : Arctrig, Theorems-MVT
% Topic      : Derivative
% Type       : Compute

\ProblemFileHeader{500}
\ifquestionPull
\ifproblemToFind\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0054. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the function $10 \, \arctan\left(-5 \, x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,5]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,5]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,5)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,5]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\frac{1}{5} \, \sqrt{\frac{25}{\arctan\left(25\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}

\begin{problem}

Does the function $9 \, \arctan\left(x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,5]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,5]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,5)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,5]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\sqrt{\frac{5}{\arctan\left(5\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}

Does the function $7 \, \arctan\left(-3 \, x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,3]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,3]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,3)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,3]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\frac{1}{3} \, \sqrt{\frac{9}{\arctan\left(9\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0054. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the function $-7 \, \arctan\left(5 \, x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,1]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,1]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,1)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,1]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{5} \, \sqrt{\frac{5}{\arctan\left(5\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0054. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the function $-2 \, \arctan\left(8 \, x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,4]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,4]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,4)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,4]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{8} \, \sqrt{\frac{32}{\arctan\left(32\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0054. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the function $-8 \, \arctan\left(-7 \, x\right)$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,1]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,1]$}
\choice{No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,1)$}
\choice{No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,1]$}
\choice[correct]{Yes, all the conditions are met}
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{\frac{7}{\arctan\left(7\right)} - 1}}\]
\end{problem}}\fi             %% end of \ifproblemToFind near top of file
\fi             %% end of \ifquestionCount near top of file
\ProblemFileFooter
